1:39:38 4 one request. 5 6 7 8 one request.
1:39:42 While in the regular way, we send one

7:22:26 this page couldn't be rendered
7:22:28 statically as it uses the cookies. That
7:22:31 means that the page or component you're
7:22:33 trying to render relies on data from

7:22:40 buildtime and cannot use runtime
7:22:43 specific features like the cookies which
7:22:45 are only available at request time. So
7:22:48 setting this export cons dynamic to
7:22:50 force dynamic will make the page render
7:22:53 on the server for each request which is
